62a5(mdo sde): chags dang / nga dang nga'ir 'dzin pa rnams bkag pa'o// dge slong mngon du bstan pa ni sems can rnams tshangs pa dang / brgya byin gyis lus la ma smin par
62a6(mdo sde): 'jig rten las 'das pa bla na med pa'i chos la brtson par bsgrub par bya'o// grong khyer mchog nas byung ste/ gshegs pa ni khams gsum gyi brtson ra las
62a7(mdo sde): thar pa dang / 'bras bu ma yin pa rnams bstan pa'o// slar gzigs pa ni byams sdang mi mnga' bar spen pa'o// de'i phyir mtshan sum cu rtsa gnyis kyi sku rnam pa
62a8(mdo sde): brgyan cing sems can gyi bsod nams kyi zhing du bya'o// dbu skra bregs pa dang / rgyan rnams spangs pa dang / rta tsan ta ka zha 'bring dad pa can la slar bskur ba'o// nyon mongs
62b1(mdo sde): ba thams cad dang bral bar bstan pa'o// kha spu bregs ni chos thams cad la mi chags bstan pa'o// ga sha dur smrig gyon pa ni sems can 'dul bar bstan pa'o//
62b2(mdo sde): drang srong mu ha ka dang / a ran ha la chos 'dri rtog bya ba ni rang gi nga rgyal gyi sems 'joms par bstan pa'o// le drug gi bar du dka' thub spyad pa ni mu steg 'dul ba'o//
62b3(mdo sde): zhal zas blangs pa ni 'jig rten pa'i chos kyi rje su 'brang ba'o// rtsa sa sti ka bslangs pa ni chos shes par bstan pa'o// rtsa snyid pa'i steng du bzhugs pa ni nyams
62b4(mdo sde): rangs dang g.yel ba rnams 'joms par bstan pa'i lha kun gyis bstod cing bsngags pa dang / bsnyen bkur bya ba ni yon tan gyis 'bras bu la bkod par bstan pa'o//
62b5(mdo sde): bdud rnams btul ba ni dpa' ba'i mthu bstan pa'o// phyag g.yas pa sa la bstan pa ni/ bsod nams kyi mthu bstan pa'o// sa chen po kun tu g.yos pa ni drin/
62b6(mdo sde): gyi lan byar bstan pa'o// de ltar mtshan ma med par bsgoms pa'i phyir/ bla na med pa'i byang chub kyi lam thob pa yin/ 'di ltar chos thams cad kyi mtshan nyid
62b7(mdo sde): mngon par mkhyen nas chos kun mnyam pa nyid du bstan pa ni/ sangs rgyas zhes bya'o// sangs rgyas kyi ye shes la thub pa me de/ chos bstan to cog la sangs rgyas su
62b8(mdo sde): 'grub pa bstan pas ni/ de bzhin gshegs pa zhes bya'o// dus gsum gyi bya ba dge ba dang mi dge ba'i chos mngon du gsal bar gzigs shing mkhyen pa ni thams cad
63a1(mdo sde): mkhyen pa zhes pa zhes bya'o// bden pa yang dag par gsung ba'i phyir/ lha dang mi'i mkhan po zhes bya'o// gang zhig de ltar brlab cing rtog pa ni byang chub
63a2(mdo sde): sems zhes bya'o// de bas log par rtog pa ni byang chub sems dpa' zhes mi bya ste/ sangs rgyas thams cad la bslu ba can zhes bya'o// rigs kyi bu sangs rgyas
63a3(mdo sde): thams cad ni mi 'byung mi 'jug mi skye mi gog ste/ sems can dmya ngan las zla ba'i phyir/ 'jig rten du 'byung ngo zhes brjod pa dang / sangs rgyas mya ngan 'das zhes
63a4(mdo sde): brjod pa yin no// de nas bcom ldan 'das la byang chub seMs dpa' na mkha'i snying pos 'di skad ces gsol to// bcom ldan 'das bdag kyang yang dag par chos thams
63a5(mdo sde): cad kyi ngo bo nyid ni stong pa nyid du rtogs te/ de bzhin gshegs pa la 'byung ba'am/ nub pa yang mi mnga' bas/ rgyal po'i pho brang du yang ma bltam/ byang chub kyi shing
63a6(mdo sde): drang du yang ma ngan las kyang ma 'das/ mtha' las 'das te yun du gnas pa'i sems can yongs su bskal bar mdzad pa'i slad da dka' thub sprad cing mya ngan las
63a7(mdo sde): 'da' bar bstan kyang / yang dag par 'gyur ba 'am/ spros pa mi mnga'/ de bzhin gshegs pa'i spyod yul yun du gnas te/ khams gsum na skra 'byung ba
63a8(mdo sde): yang chos kyi sku rnam lnga 'byung ngo // lnga po gang zhe na 'di lta ste/ sku yang dag pa'i ngo bo nyid dang / sku yon tan dang / sku chos kyi ngo bo nyid las skyes pa dang / sku sprul
63b1(mdo sde): cing 'byung ba dang / sku na mkha' lta bu dang lha ste/ de sku yang dag pa'i ngo bo nyid ces bya ba ni yang dag pa'i 'bras bu mchog mtshan ma thams cad las 'das pa rang
63b2(mdo sde): gi dbyings la yun du gnas pas na ska yang dag pa'i ngo bo nyid ces bgyi'o// ska yon tan can zhes bgyi ba ni sems can mya ngan ba zla ba'i slad du spod pa rnam pa/
63b3(mdo sde): sna tshogs mdzad cing / dge ba thams cad phun sum tshogs par mdzad pas ni/ skra yon tan can zhes bgyi'o// chos kyi skra ngo bo nyid las skyes zhes bgyi ba ni
63b4(mdo sde): chos kyi mtshan nyid thams cad thugasu chud de/ mi mkhyen pa mi mnga'/ spyod yul de yang dag par mkhyen pa'i stong pa nyid las skyes te/ yang dag par rdzogs
63b5(mdo sde): bas na/ skra chos kyi ngo bo nyid las skyes shes bgyi'o// ska sprul cing 'byung ba zhes bgyi ba ni/ de bzhin gshegs pa 'jig rten du 'byung yang lam rgyud lnga
63b6(mdo sde): dge sdig kun la mngon par bstan cing / skyabasu mi mdzad pa ma mchis/ sprul pa'i rdzas las mdzad du 'gyur bas na sku sprul cing 'byung ba zhe bgyi'o// ska
63b7(mdo sde): na mkha' lta bu zhes bgyi ba ni/ nam mkha' mtha' yas pas na chos kyi sku yang mtha' ya so// na mkha' dpag pa dang gzhal du mchis pas na chos kyi ska la yang
63b8(mdo sde): dpag cing gzhal du ma mchis te/ de bzhin gshegs pa'i sku na mkha' chen po dang 'dra bas/ sems can yongasu mya ngan las bzla ba'i slad du sku rnam pa lngar/
64a1(mdo sde): ston pas na/ de bzhin gshegs pa la skye mi mnga'/ 'gag par mi mnga' bar mngon no// chos thams cad kyang de bzhin te/ sems can yongs mya
64a2(mdo sde): ngan las bzla ba'i slad du/ sangs rgyas mchod du sprul cing chos rnam par phel ba legaso legaso// zhe gsol nas/ de nas bcom ldan 'das kyis byang chub sems dpa
64a3(mdo sde): na mkha'i snying po la 'di skad ces bka' stsal te// rigs kyi bu khyod ni de bzhin gshegs pa dang 'dra bar chos kyi mtshan nyid la mkhas pas/ spyod yul thams
64a4(mdo sde): cad la bar du chod pa 'am/ thogs pa med/ rigs kyi bu khyod ma 'ongs dus na bskal pa stong rnam par dag pa zhes bya ba dang / 'jig rten gyi khams longs spyod
64a5(mdo sde): can zhes bya ba der byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po sha dag theg pa chen po 'da' shig spyod de/ nyan thos dang spangs rgyas kyi theg pa'i ming rna ba'i thog
64a6(mdo sde): mar yang mi grags na/ ngan song lta ci zhig smos/ khyod bskal pa deng nga 'jig der de bzhin gshegs pa dgra bcom pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas rnam
64a7(mdo sde): par dag pa zhe bya ba 'byung ste/ 'jig rten nas skyes bu chen po dag kyang der phyin cing theg pa thar pa chen po phyogasu rgyas pa'i mdo sde mnyan pa dang / blang ba dang / bcang
64a8(mdo sde): bar 'gyuraro// de bas na sems can gang lus byang chub sems dpa' na mkha'i snying po'i ming thos te/ phyag 'tshal zhing mchod pa byas na 'jig rten longs spyod can
64b1(mdo sde): gyi zhing khabs der yang skyes par 'gyu po// sems can gang la las theg pa chen po'i chos sgrub na yang mi skye ba'i chos la bzod pa thob par 'gyu ro// gang chos kyi rnam
64b2(mdo sde): grang 'di blang zhing bcangs pa de ni/ sangs rgyas 'byung ba bcu ma 'das par lung bstan par yang thob par 'gyur ro// de'i tshe de'i dus na/ bcom ldan 'das shAkya thub pa la
64b3(mdo sde): byang chub sems dpa' mtshan nyid tha dad pa bdag dang sems can thams cad kyi don gyi phyir zhus nas/ bcom ldan 'das kyi phyogs bcu dus gsum gyi mtshan dang / mdo sde
64b4(mdo sde): bcu gnyis kyi mtshan dang / byang chub sems dpa' chen po'i dge 'dun rnams kyi mtshan bstan nas/ yang seng ge'i sgra chen po sgrog te// seng ge'i sgra zhes bya ba ni nges pa'i
64b5(mdo sde): tshig bstan pa'o// nges pa'i tshig bstan pa ni de bzhin gshegs pa rtag par 'tsho skyong zhing ba zhes pa/ mya ngan las 'das par rigs pa'o// yang sems can thams cad
64b6(mdo sde): las sangs rgyas kyi ngo bo nyid yod do zhes bya ba bstan pa dang / lha'i bdud dang mu stegs la sogs pa kong ste/ skyabs kyi dbang du gyur pas na seng ge'i sgra zhes bya'o//
64b7(mdo sde): de ltar bstan nas ljags kyi mtshan rgya chen pos stong gsum gyi stong chen po'i khams kun khyab par g.yog nas/ 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad rnam pa drug tu g.yoso//
64b8(mdo sde): rnam pa drug du g.yas zhes pa ni shar phyogs mthon nub phyogs dpa'/ rlung phyogs mthom shar phyogs dpa'/ lho phyogs mthon byang phyogs dpal bu phyogs mngon rtsa
65a1(mdo sde): @phyogs dpal dbus mthon mtha' das la mtha' mtshon dbus dma' ba nis rnam pa drug tu ga yos shes bya'o// sngags kyi drung nas 'od zer chen po bsan
65a2(mdo sde): ste/ phyogs bcur snang ba chen po khyab par byas so// snang ba chen po des mi rtag pa ni rtag par byas/ ma rtag pa ni dag par byas/ sdug bsngal can ni bde bar byas/ ma rig
65a3(mdo sde): pa ni rigs par byas so// de'i tshe sangs rgyas kyi 'od kyis reg cing snang ngo cog la/ ri dang nag 'tshal dang yul sa dag/ chu bo'i gling dang / rgya mtsho dang / lcags kyi ri'i
65a4(mdo sde): 'khor yug dang / dmyal ba la sogs pa thams cad kyang mthon dman med par mnyam par 'gyur te/ nya la nyil dang ldan ljin med de/ kun kyang yongasu dag par gyur nas/
65a5(mdo sde): 'di lta ste dper na/ shar phyogs na 'jig rten bzla gang rnams yongasu brgyan pa dang 'dra'o// de'i tshe de'i dus na/ bcom ldan 'das shAkya thub pa'i sku'i sprul pa na mkha'
65a6(mdo sde): nas bab pa ni me tog gi char 'bab pa dang / sa 'og nas byung ba'i sprin dang na bun byang ba dang 'dra bar na mkha' yongasu gang ste/ na mkha' stong pacud kyang me do// sprul pa'i
65a7(mdo sde): zhal so so nas tshig mthun de bzhin gshegs pa ni rtag par 'tsho skyong zhing gzhes te/ mya ngan las mi 'da'o// sems can thams cad sangs rgyas kyi ngo bo nyid yod do//
65a8(mdo sde): zhes gsung ba yang chos thams cad ni stong pa nyid do zhes gsungaso// spyod lam de dag gi rgyu dang 'bras bu'i theg pa gcig tu zad pa las sems can gyis theg pa gsum
65b1(mdo sde): du mthong ngo zhes bshad nas de ma thag tu kun mi snang bar gyur nas/ bcom ldan 'das gdan la bzhugs pa nyi tshe snang ste/ de'i tshe tshogs mang po thams cad kyi sku
65b2(mdo sde): sprul pa de dag mthong bas/ bcom ldan 'das shAkya thub pa'i byin rlabs kyi mthu ste/ shAkya thub pa yang byams pas 'dri ba'i rdzu 'phrul dang gzi brjid mngon par sprul pa
65b3(mdo sde): de'i tshogs kyi nang na byang chub sems dpa' gang ge bzhi bcu'i bye ma snyed kyis ni mi skye ba'i chos la bzod pa thob bo// nyan thos brgyad khri zhig ni theg pa chen po'i sems
65b4(mdo sde): bskyed do// dge slong phrag bcu zhig ni dgra bcom pa'i lam thob bo// dge slong ma khri brgyad stong zhig ni phyir mi 'ong ba'i lam thob po// dge bsnyen ma khri phrag bcu ni lan
65b5(mdo sde): cig phyir mi 'ongs lam thob bo// dge bsnyen ma 'bum phrag bcu zhig ni rgyun du zhugs pa'i lam thob bo// lha dang mi grangs med pa zhig ni chos kyi mig rdul med pa/
65b6(mdo sde): dri ma dang bral ba rnam par dag pa thob ste/ rang gi tshe snga phyi shes pa dang / 'dus byas kyi chos thams cad mi rtag par mthong ngo // des tshogs kyi nang nas byang chub sems/
65b7(mdo sde): dpa' chen po seng ge sgra stan las langs te/ bla gos phrag pa gcig tu gzar nas/ bcom ldan 'das kyi zhabs la btugs te phyag 'tshal nas/ bcom ldan 'das la
65b8(mdo sde): 'di skab ces gsol to// bcom ldan 'das gong du bstan pa bzhin ni/ sangs rgyas kyi mtshan thos nas yang sdig pa byang / chos kyi mtshan thos na yang sdig pa bya ba/
66a1(mdo sde): dge 'dun thos na yang sdig pa byang bar 'gyur ro zhes 'byung na sangs rgyas kyi mthu lags sam/ chos kyi mthu lags sam/ dge 'dun
66a2(mdo sde): gyi mthu lags/ sangs rgyas kyi mthu lag na ni sangs rgyas la gsol bar bgyi/ chos kyi mthu lags na ni chos la gsol bar bgyi/ dge 'dun gyi mthu lags na ni
66a3(mdo sde): dge 'dun la gsol bar bgyi lags na/ gsum car la gsol ba bgyi ba ci 'tshal/ gang nas gsungs pa theg pa cig la/ so so'i skye bos rnam pa gsum du mthong
66a4(mdo sde): ngo zhes 'byung na/ bcom ldan 'das nyid kyis kyang rnam pa gsum du bshad na sems can lha zhig ci smos zhes gsol ba dang / bcom ldan 'das kyis byang chub sems
66a5(mdo sde): dpa' sems dpa' chen po seng ge'i sgra la 'di skad ces bka' stsal to// legaso legs so rigs kyi bu sems can la phan pa dang bde ba'i phyir don de lta bu dri ba yang
66a6(mdo sde): yang shin tu legs te/ nyon cig ngas khyod la bye brag phyed par bshad do// sangs rgyas kyi mthu 'ba' zhig kyang ma yin/ chos kyi mthu 'ba' zhig kyang ma yin/ dge
66a7(mdo sde): 'dun gyi mthu 'ba' zhig kyang ma yin te/ kun tshogs pa'i mthus sangs rgyas ni sems can mgon skyabs kyi pha ma chos ni skyob par byed pa'i lam/ byang chub sems dpa'
66a8(mdo sde): ni dge ba'i bshes gzhan yin no/ sems can klad pa can sems tor ba rnyed de/ 'khor ba la skye nas dran pa'i mthu mang pos/ khams gsum nagon mongs pa'i
66b1(mdo sde): rgya mtsho las bsgral bar 'dod/ phyogs su rgyas pa'i mdo sde 'dis bsgral ba'i gru chen por byed par byed do// de bas na rigs kyi du sangs rgyas kyang chos so// chos
66b2(mdo sde): kyang dge 'dun no// dge 'dun ni 'dus ma byas pa'o// 'dus ma byas pa'o// 'dus ma byas pa ni spong ba nyid de/ 'dus ma byas stong pa nyid dang / nang stong pa nyid
66b3(mdo sde): dang / byi spong pa nyid dang / chen po stong pa nyid dang / chu ngu stong pa nyid kyang spong pa nyid du 'dra ste/ de las gzhan med do// rigs kyi bu khyod zer ba ltar na rnam
66b4(mdo sde): ba gcig tu bsgrub pa'i rigs kyi/ rnam pa gsum du bsgrub pa'i dgos pa zhes bya ba ni rigs kyi bu 'di lta ste/ dper na mi gcig cig na mkha' stong pas skrag
66b5(mdo sde): ste/ gar phyin gar gab kyang na mkha' dang yongs ma bral// rigs kyi bu phyogs bcu'i de bzhin gshegs pas bshad pa dang / ngas bshad do cog dge ba thams
66b6(mdo sde): cad kyi rgyu rkyen dang / dkon mchog gsum dang / theg pa gsum yang gcig las mi 'da'o// byang chub sems dpa' seng ge sgras gsol ba leg so legs so// /
66b7(mdo sde): bcom ldan 'das 'phags pas bstan pa ltar na bdag snga nas 'tshal to// sems can rnams kyi slad du don de zhu ba legs so// bcom ldan 'das kyis bka' stsal
66b8(mdo sde): ba/ de bzhin du mi gnyis mi gsum mo// phyogs bcu sangs rgyas kyi yum/ byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi shul chen po/ rnal 'byor pa rnams kyi mig ste/
66b9(mdo sde): chos kyi rnam grang 'di ni
67a1(mdo sde): lta ba log pa rnams bsdud pa/ sems skor ba rnams skyong ba/ ngan song gyi sgo gcod pa dang / bla na ma mchis pa'i byang chub kyi sgo 'byed
67a2(mdo sde): ba dang / nyan thos rnams bzlog ste/ theg pa chen por 'dzud pa'i srad du bdag gis gzungs chen po'i sngags kyis bskyab par bgyi'o// sdom pa nyams pa dang /
67a3(mdo sde): mdo sde 'di la bsgom zhing bslab par bgyid pa la yang bsrung zhing bskyab par bgyi'o// gal te gang la las mdo sde 'di la bsnyen bkur bgyid cing gung bdun gyi
67a4(mdo sde): bar du spyad pa sprod pa la bdud sdig can gyis 'khrug cing che ba'i grags lta ba ma mchis na/ bdud sdig can gyi glags kyis skabs mi rnyed par bgyi'o// bcom
67a5(mdo sde): ldan 'das bdag mdo sde 'di la rim gro bgyis te/ yun ring por gnas par bgyi ba yang byang chub kyi snying po la mchis kyi bar du bgyi'o// bcom ldan 'das kyis
67a6(mdo sde): bka' stsal pa/ rigs kyi bu mdo sde 'di la rim gro bya ba ni/ dkon mchog gsum la rim gro bya ba dang 'dra'o// de nas byang chub sems dpa' seng ge'i sgras/ bcom
67a7(mdo sde): ldan 'das kyi spyan sngar gzungs sngags 'di smras so// na mo bud d+hA ya/ na mo d+harma ya/ na mo sang gA ya/ a dan d+he/ d+ha ra ni/ ha thA ga a ga sha ni sa b+ha ba/
67a8(mdo sde): sarba dar mi ni/ sa ngag/ e sha me d+ha/ rdi sha na/ bi ma la su ba ri/ dang ma yi 'di kan/ ba lan lI ya ta/ mA le dz+wa la tsA le/ shu lu hu lu/ shaun+ma
67b1(mdo sde): shing+ge man tra swA hA/ sngags 'di dus cig lan brgya rtsa brgyad bzlas shing mchod rten la lan bdun bskor ba bgyi/ de ltar gdugs bdun gyi bar du mdo sde gzhan
67b2(mdo sde): mi bsam par rar gdugs gcig tu dus gsum du phyogs su rgyas pa'i mdo sde 'di la sems rtse gcig tu bgyis he/ sems gzhan du mi g.yeng bar bgyi'o// /
67b3(mdo sde): bcom ldan 'das gzungs sngags 'di ni sangs rgyas khri phrag brgyad gsungs pa te/ der 'dir bdag gis kyang brjod pa legs so// gal te 'ga' zhig
67b4(mdo sde): gzungs 'di la smod pa mchis na sangs rgyas de dag la smod par 'gyur ro// gzungs 'di la smod po ni tshe rabs du ma'i bar du byang chub bsgrub par mi 'gyur te//
67b5(mdo sde): srid pa gsum las kyang mi 'da'o// de ci'i slad du zhe na/ sngags 'di ni sems can dran pa nyams pa rnams slar rnyed par 'gyur ba dang / gzungs 'di lan
67b6(mdo sde): gcig tsam na bar thos sam/ thos nas yi ger bris te/ sha dang chang mi 'tshal bar sdom pa la gnas shing / bdag rtse 'jo la sogs spangs te/ 'du 'dzin
67b7(mdo sde): rang du mi 'jug la rgyun du byams pa chen po spyod cing / bsams gtan la gces par 'dzin na/ gang zag de dpag tu ma mchis pa'i sgrib pa gsum gyi sdig lci ba rnams
67b8(mdo sde): byang bar 'gyu ro// gzungs 'di thos ma thag tu sems thag pa nas blang ba dang / bcang ba dang nyin re bzhin klog pa dang / kha don du bgyid pa dang / yid dam du mi
68a1(mdo sde): bskyang bar bgyid na/ gang zag de mngon par byang ba chub kyi bar du ngan song gsum du lhung bar mi 'gyur ro// bcom ldan 'das kyis byang chub sems
68a2(mdo sde): dpa' seng ge'i sgra la bka' stsal pa/ legs so legs so// rigs kyi bu khyod dkon mchog gsum gyi rim gro bya ba dang / byams pa'i sems can rnams srid
68a3(mdo sde): pa gsum las gdon pa dang / bslab pa mang po grangs med pa la phan pa dang bde ba chen po bya ba'i phyir ston pa'i sgo 'byed cing log par lta ba rnams bzlog ste//
68a4(mdo sde): yang dag par lta ba la 'jud pa'i phyir gzungs sngags 'di bshad pa shin tu 'ang legs so// rigs kyi bu sems can thams cad khyod kyi ming dang / sngags kyi sgra thos
68a5(mdo sde): nas dad pa dang / gus pa skyes te mi smod na/ gang zag de'i tshe 'di nyid la yang bde/ 'chi 'phos na yang rtag tu sangs rgyas thams cad mthong zhing nga yang mthong la/
68a6(mdo sde): khyod la sogs byang chub sems dpa' thams cad kyang mthong bar 'gyur ro// mngon par 'tshangs rgya bar nges par rang gis rig ste/ the tsom med// de la 'di skad
68a7(mdo sde): ces bya ste/ kun nas nyon mongs spangs pa dang / dge ba kun gyi lam bsgrubs te/ sangs rgyas rang bzhin mthong ba yang / rnam dag dad pa'i dbang giso// yang btso//
68a8(mdo sde): ldan 'das kyis 'di skad ces bka' stsal to// nga mya ngan las 'das pa'i 'og tu rigs kyi bu 'am/ rigs kyi bu mo gang la las nyin gcig gam mtshan gcig gam/
68b1(mdo sde): skad cig ma cig la phyogs bcu dus gsum du gshegs pa'i sangs rgyas dang / mdo sde bcu gnyis dang / byang chub sems dpa'i dnga'i dge 'dun rnams la phyag
68b2(mdo sde): 'tshal zhing theg pa chen po tshul bzhin yid la byed pa dang / don dam pa'i bden pa la bsams na/ gang zag de ni skad cig ma se gol gtogs pa tsam gyis mi
68b3(mdo sde): dge ba bcu dang / mtshams med lnga dang // mnyam pa nyid la bskur ba dang / kun nas nyon mongs pa'i las thams cad yongasu ma lus par byang bar 'gyur ro// gal te
68b4(mdo sde): dge slong ngam/ dge slong ma 'am/ byang chub sems dpa' 'am/ dge sbyongs mas sems kyi rang bzhin stor nas rtsa ba bzhi dang / sdom pa brgyad nyams pa dang / mi
68b5(mdo sde): dge ba bcu dang / mtshams med pa lnga byas pa dang / mnyam pa nyid la bskur ba rnams phyogs bcu dus gsum du gshegs pa'i sangs rgyas kyi mtshan gyi mtshan la dad
68b6(mdo sde): pa bskyed de phyag 'tshal na 'di lta bu'i las ngan pa kun ma lus par byang bar 'gyur ro// de skad ces bka' stsal ma thag tu/ sngon sangs rgyas 'od mi 'gyur gyi dus na/
68b7(mdo sde): rgyal bu dge mthong bya ba de'i tshe/ mi sum stong dang lhan cig tu skad cig ma der lhags nas/ bcom ldan 'das kyi zhangs la mgo bos bzhugs te phyag 'tshal nas tshig

69a7(mdo sde): la btsugs te/ bcom ldan 'das la 'di skad ces gsol to// bcom ldan 'das bdag cag phyogs bcu'i sangs rgyas la skyabasu gsol/ phyogs bcu'i chos
69a8(mdo sde): la skyabasu 'chi'o// phyogs bcu'i dge 'dun la skyabasu 'chi'o// yang 'di lnga sde shar phyogs kyi sangs rgyas 'khrug mi mnga' la phyag 'tshal zhing skyabasu gso'o//
69b1(mdo sde): lho phyogs kyi sangs rgyas rin chen 'byung gnas la phyag 'tshal zhing skyabs su 'chi'o// nus phyogs kyi sangs rgyas 'od dpag med la phyag 'tshal zhing skyabasu gsol//
69b2(mdo sde): byang phyogs kyi sa d+yas don yod grub pa la phyag 'tshal zhing skyangs su gsol lo// bla ma phyogs kyi sangs rgyas dri brtsegs la phyag 'tshal zhing skyabasu gsol lo// 'og
69b3(mdo sde): phyogs kyi sangs rgyas gzugs rnyen 'bum la phyag 'tshal zhing skyangs su 'chi'o// yang shar phyogs kyi skyes bu chen po kun tu bzang po la phyag 'tshal zhing skyabasu gso'o//
69b4(mdo sde): lho phyogs na skye bu chen po 'jig rten lnga phyag 'tshal zhing skyabasu gsol lo// nub phyogs na skyes bu chen po kun tu spyan ras gzigs dbang byug la phyag 'tshal zhing

69b8(mdo sde): ba la bdag nyid kyang phyag 'tshal zhing skyangs su gsol lo// phyogs gzhan na yang sangs rgyas sprul pa'i sku la phyag 'tshal zhing skyabs su gsol lo//

70a7(mdo sde): bzhi dang / tshangs pa dang brgya byin dang / sum bcu rtsa gsum lha'i dbang phyug dang / bar snang na gnas pa'i lha dang / sa'i lha dang ri dang / nag tshal dang /

221a3(mdo sde): ldan 'das la mngon par bka' ste/ tshig su bcad pa 'di dag gis bcom ldan 'das la mngon par bstod do// srid pa'i rang bzhin rgyu ma'i rang bzhin rtogs mdzad
221a4(mdo sde): nas/ byed pa sgyu ma lta bur dngos po med par bston/ rgyu ma lta bu'i sems can khams ni 'dul mdzad kyang / 'di na sems can rang bzhin ma mchis
221a5(mdo sde): khams ma mchis/ dper na mi zhig gnyid kyis log pa'i rmi lam na/ gzugs mthong yang dag 'du shes de bzhin mthong ma lags/ 'das byas
221a6(mdo sde): dngos po ma mchis rmi lam 'dra bar gsungs/ chos rnams snang yang 'di ni chos la chags ma mchis/ de nas byang chub sems dpa' de dag gis byang chub
221a7(mdo sde): sems dpa'i bstod pa tshad med pa dag gis bcom ldan 'das la mngon par bsnyon nas/ nub dang / byang gi phyogs 'tshams yogs su gnas te/ rang gi rdza
221a8(mdo sde): 'phrul kyi sgrogs kyis sprul pa'i rang rang gi bstan dag la 'khod do// bcod de nas byang dang shar kyi 'tshams phyogs na/ de bzhin gshegs pa na mkha'i dkyil dri ma

221b2(mdo sde): bya ba 'od des bskul ma thag tu/ byang chub sems dpa' gang gi'i klung bcu'i bye ma snyed kyis yongasu bskor cing mdun bdar he/ lhan gcig tu sangs rgyas kyi zhing de nas mi
221b3(mdo sde): snang bar gyur nas/ skad cig thang cig yud tsam de la 'jig rten kyi mi 'byed der phyin ste/ 'khor gyi khyams rin po che bkod par/ bcom ldan 'das kyi spyan sngar 'dug nas/

221b7(mdo sde): mtha' yas blo mnga' sems kyi bsam pa cho ga mkhyen/ sems can cig gi spyod bzhin sems can kun gyi spyod/ gang dag dus gsum ldan pa de dag khod kyis mkhyen
221b8(mdo sde): sems can 'du shes mi 'jug sems kyi 'du shes min/ 'du shes yongs shes mkhas shing mnyam pa nyid dang ldan/ de nas byang chub sems dpa' de dag gis//

222a3(mdo sde): kyi sangs rgyas kyi zhing 'jig rten gyi khamams rnam par snang byed du snang ba na/ byang chub sems dpa' spobs pa'i rgyan bkod pa zhes bya ba 'od des bskul ma thag tu/

234b5(mdo sde): lus rnam par dag pa dang / ngag rnam par dag pa dang / yid rnam par dag pa ste/ gsum po 'di dag go/ rigs kyi bu byang chub sems dpa' rnams

234b7(mdo sde): thob pa dang / gang bcom pa de nyams 'og tu chung bar byed pa ste/ bzhi po 'di dag go/ rigs kyi bu byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi tshul khrims kyirgyan
234b8(mdo sde): lnga po 'di dag ste/ lnga gang zhe na/ 'di lta ste/ tshul khrims dang ldan pa'i ting nge 'dzin smra med pa yin/ shes rab sgyu med pa yin/ rnam par grol ba sgyu
235a1(mdo sde): med pa yin/ rnam par grol ba'i ye shes mthong ba sgyu med pa yin/ yongs su mya ngan las 'das pa chen po bla na med pa sgyu med pa
235a2(mdo sde): yin te/ lnga po 'di dag go/ rigs kyi bu byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi tshul khrims kyi rgyan ni drug po 'di dag ste/ drug gang zhe na/ 'di lta ste/ yid la
235a3(mdo sde): chags pa med pa'i tshul khrim kyi phyir skyon med pa'i tshul khrims dang / kha na ma tho ba med pa'i tshul khrims kyi phyir nyams pa med pa'i tshul khrims dang / 'dren pa ma
235a4(mdo sde): yin pa'i tshul khrims kyi phyir 'dres pa ma yin pa'i tshul khrims dang / dge ba'i chos shin tu rnam par 'phel ba'i phyir sra sre ma yin pa'i tshul khrims dang / gang
235a5(mdo sde): gis 'dod par 'gro ba'i tshul khrims kyi phyir rang dga'i tshul khrims dang / gzhan la rag ma las pa'i shes pa'i tshul khrims kyi phyir/ rang gis dbang sgyur ba'i
235a6(mdo sde): chu la khrims te/ drug po 'di dag go/ rigs kyi bu byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi tshul khrims kyi rgyan ni bdun po 'di dag te/ bdun gang zhe na/ 'di lha ste/

235b1(mdo sde): rnams kyi rgyan ni brgyan po 'di dag ste/ brgyad gang zhe na/ 'di sa ste/ spobs pa phun sum tshogs pa dang / sa phun sum tshogs pa dang / rnam par 'thob ma/
235b2(mdo sde): ba phun sum tshogs pa dang / lhong po med pa phun sum tshogs pa dang / khong tu 'dzin pa med pa phun sum tshogs pa dang / sangs rgyas 'byung ba mnyes par byed

235b5(mdo sde): bsam pa nges pa yin/ nye bar zhi ba yin/ bsil ba yin/ btsang ba lhod pa yin/ sems las su rung ba yin/ sems can shes pa yin/ dul ba'i sa

235b7(mdo sde): mtshan dang dpe'i byad bzang po yongasu rdzogs pa'i phyir lus phyir brgyan dang / ji skad smras pa de bzhin byed pa'i phyir dag gis rgyan dang / nyon mongs pa med pa phyir/

236a1(mdo sde): sdig pa thams cad ma byed pa'i phyir skye ba'i sman dang / de bzhin gshegs pa'i spyod pa la rjes su spongs pa'i phyir byang chub sems dpa'i spyod pa'i
236a2(mdo sde): rgyan dang / nga rgyal song ba'i phyir shes pa'i rgyan dang / dge ba'i rtsa ba yongasu snga ba'i phyir byang chub kyi snying po'i rgyan dang / tshul khrims kyi rtsa ba la gnas pa ma
236a3(mdo sde): 'dor ba'i phyir stongs dang / mi 'jig pa dang / sangs rgyas kyi chos ma 'dres pa'i rgyan ste/ rigs kyi bu bcu po 'di dag ni byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi tshul khrim
236a4(mdo sde): kyi brgyan no// rigs kyi bu byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi ting nge 'dzin kyi rgyan gang zhe na/ rigs kyi bu byang chub sems dpa' rnams rgyan ni cig ste/ gcig

236b6(mdo sde): 'di dag go/ rigs kyi bu byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi ting nge 'dzin kyi rgyan ni bdun po 'di dag ste/ bdun gang zhe na/ 'di lta ste/ byang chub kyi sems mi

236b8(mdo sde): 'grus yang dag byang chub kyi yan lag dang / dga' ba yang dag byang chub kyi yan lag dang / shin tu sbyangs pa'i yang dag byang chub kyi yan lag dang / ting nge//

237a3(mdo sde): 'di ltar yang dag par lta ba dang / yang dag pa'i rtogs pa dang / yang dag pa'i ngag dang / yang dag pa'i las kyi mtha' dang / yang dag pa'i mtsho ba dang /

237b1(mdo sde): ba'i dga' ba dang / bde ba can bsam gtan gnyis pa rdzogs par byas te gnas so// de dga' ba'i 'dod chags dang bral bas/ btang snyoms la gnas shing //
237b2(mdo sde): dran pa dang shes bzhin can yin te/ bde lus kyis myong la/ 'phags pa rnams kyis gang de dran pa dang ldan pa/ bde ba la gtang snyoms pa'o// zhes brjod
237b3(mdo sde): pa ste/ dga' ba med pa'i bsam gtan gsum pa rdzogs par byas te gnaso// de bde ba spangs te snga nas sdug bsngal yang spangs shing yid bde ba dang yid mi
237b4(mdo sde): bde ba yang nub pas/ bde ba yang ma yin sdug bsngal yang ma yin pa/ btang snyoms dang / dran pa yongs su dag pa/ bsam gtan bzhi rdzogs par byas te/
237b5(mdo sde): gnas so// de rnas pa thams cad du gzugs kyi 'du shes rnams las yang dag par 'das te/ thogs pa'i 'du shes rnams nub par gyur cing / sna tshogs kyi

242b3(mdo sde): yin te/ shes rab rnam grol de bzhin ye shes mthong / de yi mya ngan 'das pa sgyu ma yin/ 'di ni tshul khrims rnam par dag pa'i rgyan/ tshul khrims skyon med tshul

243a1(mdo sde): ni de'i bcings pa lhod par gyur/ 'di ni gang dag tshul khrims dag pa'i rgyan/ grags chen sems ni las su rung ba yin/ de ni dul zhing de bzhin cang /
